5d:["$","h2",null,{"children":"JSON Schema vs Zod: Dual-Track Parameter Validation"}]
5e:["$","p",null,{"children":"This is an interesting design divergence in Claude Code's tool system. Built-in tools use Zod Schema, while MCP tools use JSON Schema — two systems running in parallel."}]
5f:["$","h3",null,{"children":"The Zod Path for Built-in Tools"}]
60:["$","p",null,{"children":["Built-in tools (like Read, Write, Bash) define ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"inputSchema"}]," as a Zod Schema:"]}]
62:["$","p",null,{"children":"Zod Schemas are automatically converted to JSON Schema before being sent to the API."}]
63:["$","h3",null,{"children":"JSON Schema Pass-Through for MCP Tools"}]
64:["$","p",null,{"children":["MCP tools bypass the Zod layer entirely. The ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"Tool"}]," interface specifically defines an ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"inputJSONSchema"}]," field:"]}]
67:["$","p",null,{"children":["In ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"fetchToolsForClient"}],", the MCP tool's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"inputSchema"}]," (JSON Schema from the Server) is directly assigned to ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"inputJSONSchema"}],":"]}]
69:["$","p",null,{"children":"Why not convert JSON Schema to Zod? Three reasons:"}]
6a:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Performance"}],": Runtime conversion from JSON Schema to Zod has overhead, and MCP Servers may provide complex nested Schemas"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fidelity"}],": Certain JSON Schema features (",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"patternProperties"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"additionalProperties"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"oneOf"}]," combinations) have no direct Zod equivalents"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Unnecessary"}],": The Claude API itself accepts JSON Schema, so no intermediate conversion is needed"]}],"\n"]}]
6b:["$","p",null,{"children":["This is why MCPTool's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"inputSchema"}]," is a permissive ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"z.object({}).passthrough()"}]," — it performs no actual validation at runtime, and the real Schema is passed through to the API via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"inputJSONSchema"}],"."]}]

ba:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Architecture Summary"}]
bb:["$","p",null,{"children":["Claude Code's MCP integration is a carefully designed extensible architecture. It cleanly separates \"connection management\" from \"tool adaptation\": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"client.ts"}]," handles establishing and maintaining connections to MCP Servers, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"MCPTool.ts"}]," provides the tool template, and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"fetchToolsForClient"}]," bridges the two — from a Server's raw capability declarations to Tool objects callable by Claude, passing through name normalization, description truncation, Schema pass-through, permission configuration, and a series of other transformations."]}]
bc:["$","p",null,{"children":"Core principles of the overall design:"}]
bd:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Lazy discovery"}],": Only connect to Servers and fetch tool lists when needed, using memoize caching to avoid redundant operations"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Graceful degradation"}],": Connection failures don't block the entire system — only that Server's tools become unavailable; Servers requiring authentication register an ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"McpAuthTool"}]," to guide users through authentication"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Dual-track Schema"}],": Built-in tools use Zod for type safety and validation, while MCP tools use JSON Schema pass-through for flexibility and efficiency"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Defensive design"}],": From Unicode sanitization to description truncation, from configuration hash comparison to authentication cache serialization, edge case considerations are evident throughout"]}],"\n"]}]
be:["$","p",null,{"children":"For projects looking to build similar extension systems, the MCP integration provides a referenceable pattern: use template objects + object spread for dynamic tool registration, memoize caching for connection lifecycle management, union types for precise connection state expression, and configuration hierarchies for flexible scope management."}]
